  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_a4a12e39-cff8-4782-84b7-5fc9f197e30d'
      });
    }

      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"

  <span id="freeText15265104609576988973" style="display:none">Demi Lovato wakes up each morning and affirms her commitment to herself—to her health, her happiness, her being. Those commitments are the bedrock of her recovery and her work helping other young people dealing with the issues she lives with every single day. <br /><br />Demi is a platinum-selling recording artist whose latest album—DEMI—is already a smash hit. She’s about to embark on her second season as a judge on X-Factor, and just launched The Lovato Treatment Scholarship Program. And she is an outspoken advocate for young people everywhere. <br /><br />Demi is also a young woman finding her way in the world. She has dealt deftly with her struggles in the face of public scrutiny, and she has always relied, not just on friends and family, but daily affirmations of her self-worth and value. Affirmations that steady her days and strengthen her resolve. <br /><br />Those affirmations have grown into STAYING STRONG, a powerful 365-day collection of Demi’s most powerful, honest, and hopeful insights. Each day will provide the readers with a quote, a personal reflection and a goal. <br /><br />These are Demi’s words. Words she lives by and shares with the people she loves and total strangers alike. They are a powerful testament to a young woman standing up and fighting back.</span>

<div id="review_782640055" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/782640055" />
    <a title="Elle" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5713165-elle"><img alt="Elle" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1397319053p2/5713165.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/782640055?book_show_action=true">Dec 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elle" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elle" href="/user/show/5713165-elle">Elle</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="ebook 9781466854154" href="/book/show/18462260-staying-strong">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5713165-elle?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer782640055" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11846954788627519432">There are not a lot of reviews for this book yet and most of them are from fans, so I'm probably going to be the odd one out, but I did not like this book. I know absolutely nothing about Demi Lovato, I've only seen her in one episode of Glee. The only reason I chose to read this was that it was featured one of my favorite book-buying sites and I could use something inspirational. Well, this didn't inspire me at all. I'm not saying that there aren't any good messages in this book, but it's 365 p</span>
  <span id="freeText11846954788627519432" style="display:none">There are not a lot of reviews for this book yet and most of them are from fans, so I'm probably going to be the odd one out, but I did not like this book. I know absolutely nothing about Demi Lovato, I've only seen her in one episode of Glee. The only reason I chose to read this was that it was featured one of my favorite book-buying sites and I could use something inspirational. Well, this didn't inspire me at all. I'm not saying that there aren't any good messages in this book, but it's 365 pages filled with quotes based on only a few ideas (and most of them are cliches). It's a lot of 'follow your dreams', 'appreciate your loved ones', 'what doesn't kill you makes you stronger'. Not very lifechanging for me. I didn't read this the way you are supposed too (one page a day), I read it per month. I can't help but feeling that if I did read one page a day I would be very dissatisfied, because you only get one quote, then a few sentences of explanation (and these explanations are mostly the same) and some vague goal-activities you can work on. One last thing: it annoys me that not every quote is paired with an author (I assume the ones that don't have a name under it are from Lovato herself? Not clear on that). There's also a famous quote from Gandhi stated as 'unknown'. So, in conclusion, I guess this book is for the fans. </span>
  <a data-text-id="11846954788627519432" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_808014905" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/808014905" />
    <a title="Evey" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/19222970-evey"><img alt="Evey" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1417196082p2/19222970.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/808014905?book_show_action=true">Jan 01, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Evey" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Evey" href="/user/show/19222970-evey">Evey</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19222970-evey?shelf=2015-reading-challenge">2015-reading-challenge</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19222970-evey?shelf=burn-them">burn-them</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19222970-evey?shelf=wtf-did-i-just-read">wtf-did-i-just-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19222970-evey?shelf=burn-book-list">burn-book-list</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19222970-evey?shelf=craptastic">craptastic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/19222970-evey?shelf=2015-pop-sugar-challenge">2015-pop-sugar-challenge</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer808014905" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16520386622201319787"><b>1 HAIL-TO-THE-NO stars</b><br/><br/>This wasn't inspiring. This wasn't helpful. This wasn't meaningful. This was, at last, infuriating.<br/><br/>I have nothing against Demi Lovato. In fact, from time to time I listen to her music. I know about her story, and it's good to know she's getting over it. But some things in this book pissed me off way too much.<br/><br/>For starters, Coelho, Miley Cyrus, Eminem and Lil Wayne as source from inspirational quotes for this type of book... Is this even serious? Mixed with Jane Austen, among</span>
  <span id="freeText16520386622201319787" style="display:none"><b>1 HAIL-TO-THE-NO stars</b><br /><br />This wasn't inspiring. This wasn't helpful. This wasn't meaningful. This was, at last, infuriating.<br /><br />I have nothing against Demi Lovato. In fact, from time to time I listen to her music. I know about her story, and it's good to know she's getting over it. But some things in this book pissed me off way too much.<br /><br />For starters, Coelho, Miley Cyrus, Eminem and Lil Wayne as source from inspirational quotes for this type of book... Is this even serious? Mixed with Jane Austen, amongst others? Well, no. I can't take that seriously. I just can't, especially if all I see in my mind is Miley's twerking on the video from the song her quote was extracted from (<i>We can't stop</i>, in case you were wondering.)<br /><br />Then, to put it nice, the entire book was absurd. It consists in a bunch of quotes with little explanations that add nothing relevant and a diary goal that, in most cases, is almost absurd as well. What makes it worse is the fact that the quotes, explanations and goals are as repetitive as I could never imagine it'd be possible. You can sum up this book in "You're such a special being, CARPE DIEM, my darling." And that's pretty much it. <br /><br />But then, what bothered me the most, was a message that appeared more than once about bullies. I suffered from bullying for years, but the worst I had to go through was when I was just nine years old. I was epileptic then, and the things I had to put up with made my seizures come back in spite of the high dose of medicine I was taking back then. In fact, I had to get my dose readjusted several times because of it. I still suffer from the psychological effects and impact bullying left at such a young age. It still hurts and it still makes me cry, not only me but also my mum. So when I read that I have to get past what I've been through by JUSTIFYING bullying, I just can't take it. Telling me that I have to forgive is one thing. Telling me that I have to forgive those who hurt me (and were completely aware about it, knew how much it affected me and they only made it worse) because "they are flawed and were probably suffering more than you" is a complete different thing. So, just because they were supposedly suffering that gives them the right to turn my life into Hell? NICE! Why didn't anybody tell me that before? That means that I can go and ruin someone else's life just because I'm suffering.<br /><br />Let me tell you one thing: IT DOESN'T MATTER WHAT YOU WENT THROUGH IN LIFE, NOTHING GIVES YOU THE RIGHT TO HURT PEOPLE IN ANY WAY. <b>NOTHING.</b><br /><br />I went through psychological and physical abuse when I was nine (and later on). I went through sexual abuse when I was even younger. You can't even imagine how much pain that causes, unless you've been through the same. <i>You can't even imagine.</i> Fear, suffering, shame, emptiness, depression, self hatred. I was nine and I cried myself to sleep. I was nine and I feared going to school. I was nine and I had to spend a whole class with ice on my face because they punched me that hard my cheek was almost violet. I was nine and I found myself on a corridor half naked because they decided it was a good idea to pull me on a tight grasp and lift up my skirt so everybody could see my underwear.<br /><br />You know what my teacher did? Nothing. Even worse: she defended the agressor.<br />You know what the director did? Nothing, but telling me I had a "little-star-know-it-all" complex.<br />You know who I was? A little girl that was /that/ terrified that hid on breaks. I was the new girl and while the "popular" clique decided they hated me, almost all the other kids decided that too. That happened the very same day school started.<br /><br />Mum had reunions with the directives, with teachers, with everybody. She called many parents to talk about it. What parents did? Defending their children, in spite of all the evidence they had against their children's behavior. They blamed me. And what did I do? I'm still asking myself that, because I don't know. And I don't want to play the victim role, but that is exactly what I was. A victim.<br /><br />They were not suffering. They were happy kids, with no family problems and no monetary problems. I had them, as my mum lost her job that year, and we were just alone. Now tell me again: they were the real victims? They were suffering and that's why they did that to me? They even insulted my mum when <i>she was right in front of them</i>.<br /><br />To sum it up, the message is terrible. TERRIBLE in every way possible. You CAN'T justify this type of abuse by saying <i>they were probably suffering too</i>. THAT'S JUSTIFYING IT. THAT'S EXACTLY WHAT YOU MUST NOT DO. You tell me to "pity them because they were obviously suffering." (I read a translated version, so I'm not sure if it's 100% accurate but it said that.) REALLY?<br /><br />I had the <i>disgust</i> to meet some of them again. It's not like they ever said they were sorry. In fact, they showed nothing but scorn. And I'm supposed to pity them?<br /><br /><i>Guess what: NO.</i><br /><br />And sorry for the long rant but it really pissed me off. It really angered me and of course I wouldn't recommend this to anyone.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="16520386622201319787" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

I'm grateful for Demi Lovato and what she has done has been so helpful and inspirational and I couldn't have asked for a better role model!<br />If you're looking for a book that will boost your confidence and just help you get through the day, I recommend this book!   <span id="freeText2789201849329891275" style="display:none">Live life to the full, one day at a time.<br>Every day read a page of <i>Demi’s</i> book and you will gain clarity, strength and internal enrichment.<br><br><i>”Be grateful for your journey because It is yours alone”</i> <br><br>Demi Lovato has had her fair share of trials, ups and downs within her life; from fighting addiction, eating disorders, depression and many other heart breaking losses. Amongst her dazzling achievements alongside an impressive singing career, she has chronicled her journey in song lyrics and media. Turning everything she has learned into a daily guide, so as to give hope and guidance to many. This profoundly candid, illuminating and uplifting book (full of inspirational and motivational quotes and tips, personal reflections and goals), is simply sublime. <br><br>Regardless of whatever personal journey you may be on, I would highly value this comforting read of impacting implication.   <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1913554064?book_show_action=true">Feb 17, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Zahraa Maytham" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Zahraa Maytham" href="/user/show/39374096-zahraa-maytham">Zahraa Maytham</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1913554064" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer943995528008122091">I was planning on reading a page each day for the rest of the year but I just couldn't stand it and I had to finish it so I won't bother myself to open and read another stupid phrase.<br/><br/>I really think there should be some rules in publishing books. One of them must be not to publish diaries of uneducated 6 year olds. Another one is not to publish something similar to a diary of a 6 year old (this book will be included in this rule). <br/><br/>Self-help books should be written by people who are experienced an</span>
  <span id="freeText943995528008122091" style="display:none">I was planning on reading a page each day for the rest of the year but I just couldn't stand it and I had to finish it so I won't bother myself to open and read another stupid phrase.<br /><br />I really think there should be some rules in publishing books. One of them must be not to publish diaries of uneducated 6 year olds. Another one is not to publish something similar to a diary of a 6 year old (this book will be included in this rule). <br /><br />Self-help books should be written by people who are experienced and specialists and not by teenage drama queens, and famous people shouldn't use their fame to publish anything and expect their fans to like it no matter what. I'm pretty sure all those 5 stars reviews are from her fans, otherwise the book added nothing new. <br /><br />The book consisted of 365 pages of "lights at the end of the tunnel, everyone is beautiful and forgive your enemies."<br />And the kind of advices that are not even practical in real life like hug your bully, or when you feel sad start filling your gratitude notebook. Like, seriously?<br /><br />Also, there was an awful combination in the quotes she mentioned. There was Lil Wayne quotes next to Nelson Mandela, and Miley Cyrus next to The Bible. I'm not even sure Demi understood the quotes cause the explanations she wrote below them had nothing to do with the quote.<br /><br />I don't hate Demi, but she shouldn't have published this book, or any book since there's no sense of literacy in it. If her intention was to help others who are dealing with what she dealt with, that's what her voice is there for. There's no need to have it all.</span>

<div id="review_771399201" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/771399201" />
    <a title="Daleen" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9281883-daleen"><img alt="Daleen" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1488583911p2/9281883.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/771399201?book_show_action=true">Nov 22, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Daleen" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Daleen" href="/user/show/9281883-daleen">Daleen</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9781250051448" href="/book/show/18462287-staying-strong">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9281883-daleen?shelf=non-fiction">non-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer771399201" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17671508776605395041">Demi Lovato is a really big inspiration of mine. Her rise to stardom, her fade, and her rise again was always something that I think makes Lovato a hero. I've always looked up to her and strive to be more like her so when she released a book about her struggles, I was insanely excited. But a book full of quotes was not what I was looking for.<br/><br/>I was hoping for something more on her actual struggle and journey with her addictions, more in an autobiographical sense, but this book is literally made u</span>
  <span id="freeText17671508776605395041" style="display:none">Demi Lovato is a really big inspiration of mine. Her rise to stardom, her fade, and her rise again was always something that I think makes Lovato a hero. I've always looked up to her and strive to be more like her so when she released a book about her struggles, I was insanely excited. But a book full of quotes was not what I was looking for.<br /><br />I was hoping for something more on her actual struggle and journey with her addictions, more in an autobiographical sense, but this book is literally made up of quotes and little blurbs about how she takes the quote. And her writing isn't really that great. It sound like she was assigned to write an essay for each quote and decided to wait until the last minute to do it.<br /><br />Her advice was almost hypocritical. On one page she would say to continue to follow your dreams but a handful of pages later say not to daydream about the future. She always gives goals for each of the days, and those are anything but goals. One for example said "The next time a friend or family member shares good news with you, make sure you joy is sincere." How can you make your emotions sincere. If you don't feel joyish about it, then how can you make sure you feel that way.<br /><br />And also, anytime you make Miley Cyrus seem like a good person by quoting one of the few "semi-inspirational" things she says, then that's a big minus for me.<br /><br />I think Lovato had good intentions but didn't carry it out as well as she should of. Maybe she should have spent more time with it instead of rushing to release it or she should have taken a different approach. Though a lot of what she says is incredibly inspiring, and the cover is absolutely goregous, and I will always love Lovato for her strength and story that she has shared, this is just not a good book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17671508776605395041" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_2479550639" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/2479550639" />
    <a title="Brianna" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/35268971-brianna"><img alt="Brianna" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1527452451p2/35268971.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/2479550639?book_show_action=true">Aug 13, 2018</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Brianna" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Brianna" href="/user/show/35268971-brianna">Brianna</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audio CD 9781427251428" href="/book/show/19286639-staying-strong">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35268971-brianna?shelf=audio-books">audio-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/35268971-brianna?shelf=read-and-reviewed">read-and-reviewed</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer2479550639" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3683549676776709355">I wanted to pick up this novel because of the recent news on Demi Lovato and her apparent overdose. I've always liked Demi Lovato and her music/acting well enough. I like the fact that she is transparent with her fans and well they may not know everything that is going on in her life, she does not shy away from her mistakes. I think she is a beautiful person inside and out, despite her faults.<br/><br/>This novel on the other hand? It felt like one of those 365-day calendars where you rip off each day for</span>
  <span id="freeText3683549676776709355" style="display:none">I wanted to pick up this novel because of the recent news on Demi Lovato and her apparent overdose. I've always liked Demi Lovato and her music/acting well enough. I like the fact that she is transparent with her fans and well they may not know everything that is going on in her life, she does not shy away from her mistakes. I think she is a beautiful person inside and out, despite her faults.<br /><br />This novel on the other hand? It felt like one of those 365-day calendars where you rip off each day for another motivational quote. Sure, you may get to know Demi a little bit better through some of the quote explanations, but for the most part it felt like journal entries to remind her to think positive.<br /><br />The one good thing about this - I listened to it instead of reading it. It helped to turn off my brain and just zone out. I'm getting married in less than a week and I keep thinking of all the things that still need to be done every moment that my brain is not occupied with something else. I could put this on and just stop thinking! But, it never would of held my attention if I had to sit down and read it.<br /><br /><b>Rated 1/5 stars - Would not recommend. </b></span>
  <a data-text-id="3683549676776709355" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<span id="freeTextContainer8723511835431887427">I liked it!<br/>It has a lot of good sayings and some stories form Demi's life. It's super inspirational, but there is one bad thing about it. You can't read it page after page. You just can't, otherwise the whole point of the book is gone. So the easiest solution is to read one page each day, keeping it in your mind through this day, but obviously after few weeks (or sooner) you'd</span>
  <span id="freeText8723511835431887427" style="display:none">I liked it!<br />It has a lot of good sayings and some stories form Demi's life. It's super inspirational, but there is one bad thing about it. You can't read it page after page. You just can't, otherwise the whole point of the book is gone. It has 365 pages of thoughts and you can't jump from one thought to another, because you need to think through it first. So the easiest solution is to read one page each day, keeping it in your mind through this day, but obviously after few weeks (or sooner) you'd get bored with it. Another solution is to read a random saying every time you want to have one. But you will not be done with the book in a year.<br />I had this book as a gift and I started reading it in January, I was done with the first part in a day, but then I got bored of wise thoughts. The whole point of these wise thoughts was to keep them in your heart, and not to read them all in one day. So I started reading 10 pages every now and then, and today I finished.<br />I liked it. It's inspirational, but I am kind of relieved that I am done with it, because I hate reading one book for several months.</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17661091238263189296">Staying Strong: 365 Days a Year is Demi's way of trying to help. She gives us insight into her struggling and what it was like overcoming self-harm along with addiction. Start each day with a quote to get through the day. Know that nothing can harm you, but yourself and the thoughts you're having. Demi Lovato wholeheartedly put her entire soul into this book. She wants young girls to have a role model. In all honest, this is a feel good kind of book. Almost everyone can relate to the things she'</span>
  <span id="freeText17661091238263189296" style="display:none">Staying Strong: 365 Days a Year is Demi's way of trying to help. She gives us insight into her struggling and what it was like overcoming self-harm along with addiction. Start each day with a quote to get through the day. Know that nothing can harm you, but yourself and the thoughts you're having. Demi Lovato wholeheartedly put her entire soul into this book. She wants young girls to have a role model. In all honest, this is a feel good kind of book. Almost everyone can relate to the things she's saying. Whether you've been bullied or not bullied, you need to read this book. We as people need to stop the hatred and violence going on in the world. We may not be able to do this one by one, but it's a start. Demi wants all of you to know that she is there for you, as do I. If anyone ever needs a shoulder to cry on, or someone to confide in, I will be here for you. Feel free to reach out to me, I'll be there for you 100% of the time. <br /><br />This was taken straight off of my book blog, A Reader's Diary. Feel free to check it out: areadersdiary1.blogspot.com </span>

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('nxC2aC5TVCew94mYutNvX+6pJ9xVhQkVGD2c6i63910AnCTwW1mKe2CVzLCNa8jYom5u2brgrBfQCtuxzdlETw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('lDRQMQxKWlIX6zUDUqtthp0gQfVFd2awddp04XOHBYYLuMKpeUCEDseJcCtlE8oB0ecI8KoSw7K97TO6kOm2lA==')})
  }

<span id="freeTextContainer450851168461371446">Demetria Devonne "Demi" Lovato (born August 20, 1992) is an American actress and singer-songwriter. She is best known for her role as Mitchie Torres in the Disney Channel Original Movie Camp Rock and Sonny Monroe in Sonny With A Chance. Besides acting, she is also a solo music artist and released her debut album Don't Forget on September 23, 2008. The album debuted at #2 on the Billboard 200 selli</span>
  <span id="freeText450851168461371446" style="display:none">Demetria Devonne "Demi" Lovato (born August 20, 1992) is an American actress and singer-songwriter. She is best known for her role as Mitchie Torres in the Disney Channel Original Movie Camp Rock and Sonny Monroe in Sonny With A Chance. Besides acting, she is also a solo music artist and released her debut album Don't Forget on September 23, 2008. The album debuted at #2 on the Billboard 200 selling over 89,000 copies in the first week. Lovato released her second album, Here We Go Again, on July 21, 2009. The album debuted at #1 on the Billboard 200 selling over 108,000 copies in the first week. </span>
